posted:Posted October 6, 2023
msg:Prices everywhere will increase during the National Day holiday. Because Longkou is far away from major scenic spots, it is actually a very cost-effective choice for self-driving.
When I checked in at the front desk, I was upgraded to Youxiang. I asked about the difference. The room type remained the same, but various small things inside had been upgraded, including the mattress. The following comments are for reference.
Letâ€™s talk about the advantages first:
1. The room is clean and the equipment is new. I think it's better than many five-star hotels I've stayed in that have been open for more than five years. I felt very comfortable as soon as I entered. For this advantage, this hotel is highly recommended.
2. Minibar and welcome fruits. Very plus point. Some five-star hotels don't have these rooms even if they don't have executive-level rooms.
3. Service attitude. Needless to say, after adding hotel Yanyanâ€™s WeChat account, basically all reasonable requests are answered, and the response speed is fast enough. Robots are more efficient in delivering and picking up things.
4. High cost performance. Normally it's only over 300, but if it doubles on November 1, it's only over 600. It takes about 40 minutes to drive to Penglai Pavilion. If you get up early, you'll have everything. Breakfast was only 30, but because we left early, we didnâ€™t try it. Small tip: Booking in advance with Co-Cheng is more expensive, but traveling on the same day is cheaper. Maybe itâ€™s cheaper to call the hotel front desk.
5. Air conditioning. I will talk about this separately, because the air conditioner really has no sound or smell. This is actually quite rare, and I hope it can be maintained.
6. The mattress and bedding are all good, and I slept well and comfortably.
Not to mention the shortcomings:
1. There is a slight problem with sound insulation. The bedroom may be next to the shower room in the next room. You can clearly hear the sound of the shower next to you in the middle of the night. This could be better.
2. It would be better if there is a swimming pool.

msg:This is my second time staying at this hotel. The first time I thought it was okay. There are no five-star hotels in Longkou, so I chose this hotel for the second time. Unexpectedly, it was not pleasant at all. I checked in early in the morning because I wanted to sleep more, so I used Ctrip. My points can be used to delay check-out until two o'clock. Nowadays, hotels have check-out at two o'clock. I don't know why this hotel is not the same. I admit it. I will use my Ctrip points to exchange for the head office. It will be available before ten o'clock in the morning. The waiter knocked on the door and said something about disinfecting the room. At 11 o'clock, the front desk called me to ask if I could extend my stay. If I didn't extend my stay, they asked me what time to check out. The room was too dry and there was no water. I asked for two bottles of mineral water. The front desk said it would be charged. Just now By two o'clock, I was ready to check out, so I called again to remind me. I have stayed in so many hotels, including the super five-star Hanbi Tower, the Ritz-Carlton, the JW Marriott, and the St. Regis. None of them are so busy. Not to mention these five-star hotels, there are also 4-star brands, and there are no other hotels. I have never met such a weird person like you.
